Q1 — How many occurrences are on GBIF?

After filtering to kingdom Plantae, Christopher Davidson’s GBIF download contains 26562 occurrences.

Each occurrence is directly accessible at https://www.gbif.org/occurrence/<gbifID>.

The vast majority of occurrences come from TROPICOS and RSA - California Botanic Garden Herbarium (21060 combined). TROPICOS also acts as a data aggregator: 9436 occurrences are listed there but not physically deposited at MO.

Q8 — Linking FotW images with SRP specimens

SRP specimen images are not on GBIF but are accessible via the Consortium of Pacific Northwest Herbaria. The local file Consortium_PacificNorthWest_herbaria/CPNWH_20250520-112502.csv lists all Davidson SRP collections with their accession numbers and an Imaged? flag.

Image URL pattern (accession must be zero-padded to 6 digits):

https://www.pnwherbaria.org/images/jpeg.php?Image=SRP<ACCESSION>.jpg
# Example: https://www.pnwherbaria.org/images/jpeg.php?Image=SRP034726.jpg

Q9 — Overlap between FotW and GBIF

Records are matched on a composite key: numeric record number + collection date (e.g., 12687_2014-10-04).

874 GBIF occurrences correspond to 468 unique FotW records.
